\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Fortran API functions for MMGS library. 

\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Author}
Algiane Froehly (Inria/\+UBordeaux) 
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxyVersion}{Version}
5 
\end{DoxyVersion}
\begin{DoxyDate}{Date}
01 2014 
\end{DoxyDate}
\begin{DoxyCopyright}{Copyright}
GNU Lesser General Public License. 
\end{DoxyCopyright}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Please, refer to the \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgs_8h}{mmgs/libmmgs.\+h}} file for functions documentation.
\end{DoxyNote}
Define the Fortran API functions for MMGS library\+: adds function definitions with upcase, underscore and double underscore to match any fortran compiler. 

Definition in file \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functionsf__s_8c_source}{API\+\_\+functionsf\+\_\+s.\+c}}.
